\DoxyCodeLine{01705\ \ \ \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01707\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keyword}{new}\ std::string((\mbox{\hyperlink{classtesting_1_1Message}{Message}}()\ <<\ name\ <<\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}="{}}\ <<\ value).GetString());}
\DoxyCodeLine{01708\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01709\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ standard\ signature\ of\ putenv\ accepts\ a\ 'char*'\ argument.\ Other}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01711\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ We\ cast\ away\ the\ 'const'\ since\ that\ would\ work\ for\ both\ variants.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01712\ \ \ putenv(\textcolor{keyword}{const\_cast<}\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*\textcolor{keyword}{>}(added\_env[name]-\/>c\_str()));}
\DoxyCodeLine{01713\ \ \ \textcolor{keyword}{delete}\ prev\_env;}
